 2914 |  1  tkdemo.s   2051 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * Many of the tool kit calls require that the mouse
 2915 |  1  tkdemo.s   2052 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * coordinates be passed back to the tool kit. Since
 2916 |  1  tkdemo.s   2053 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * the mouse coordinates are originally provided in
 2917 |  1  tkdemo.s   2054 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * the event parameters, using the same memory to pass

 2921 |  1  tkdemo.s   2058 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * Below I equate many labels to the same memory. When
 2922 |  1  tkdemo.s   2059 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * I use them in the code I try to indicate (in a comment
 2923 |  1  tkdemo.s   2060 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * that they refer to this shared area).

 2925 |  1  tkdemo.s   2062 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | *
 2926 |  1  tkdemo.s   2063 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * The event parameter is five bytes long. The first byte
 2927 |  1  tkdemo.s   2064 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/18F6               | * is the event type.  The remaining bytes depend on the
